# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

Perfect! I've completed the comprehensive analysis of etcd-io/etcd's MVCC compaction and watch stream cancellation implementation. The answer includes:

## Summary

I've identified and documented **13 key Go source files** that implement MVCC compaction in etcd:

### Core Compaction Components:

1. **Compaction Scheduling**:
   - `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/periodic.go` - Time-based periodic compaction (hourly default with 1/10th interval sampling)
   - `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/revision.go` - Revision-based compaction (every 5 minutes)
   - `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/compactor.go` - Factory and interface definitions

2. **Compaction Execution**:
   - `server/storage/mvcc/index.go` - Tree index compaction of revision indices
   - `server/storage/mvcc/kvstore_compaction.go` - Batch deletion of compacted key-value pairs from the backend
   - `server/storage/mvcc/kvstore.go` - Main Compact() method and scheduling logic

3. **Watch Stream Handling**:
   - `server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go` - Core watch stream lifecycle management with synced/unsynced watcher tracking
   - `server/storage/mvcc/watcher_group.go` - Watcher selection and compaction notification logic (chooseAll() method)
   - `server/storage/mvcc/watcher.go` - Watcher interface definitions with CompactRevision field

4. **Slow Watch Detection**:
   - `server/storage/mvcc/metrics.go` - slowWatcherGauge metric tracking unsynced slow watchers
   - Victim batch processing in watchable_store.go for blocked channels

The answer is now available at `/workspace/answer.json` with detailed files, symbols, execution chain, and narrative explanation of how these components work together.

\"server/storage/mvcc/watcher_group.go\", \"symbol\": \"chooseAll\"},\n    {\"repo\": \"github.com/etcd-io/etcd\", \"path\": \"server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go\", \"symbol\": \"syncWatchers\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"etcd's MVCC compaction system implements sophisticated management of key-value history and watch stream lifecycle through several key components:\\n\\n## Compaction Schedule (Periodic vs Revision-Based)\\n\\nThe compaction strategy is configured and managed through `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/` package with two modes:\\n\\n1. **Periodic Compaction** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/periodic.go`): The `Periodic` compactor runs at configurable time intervals (default hourly). It maintains a sliding window of revisions recorded every 1/10th of the compaction period and compacts using the oldest revision in the window. The `Run()` method starts a goroutine that records revisions periodically and triggers compaction when the retention period is reached.\\n\\n2. **Revision-Based Compaction** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/revision.go`): The `Revision` compactor triggers every 5 minutes by comparing current revision minus a retention number. The `Run()` method executes compaction when `currentRev - retentionCount > previousRev`.\\n\\nBoth are initialized by `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/compactor.go`'s `New()` function, which is called during server startup in `server/etcdserver/server.go` when `AutoCompactionRetention` is configured.\\n\\n## Compaction of Revision Indices\\n\\nThe actual compaction process involves two layers:\\n\\n1. **Key Index Compaction** (`server/storage/mvcc/index.go`): The `treeIndex.Compact(rev)` method iterates through all keys and removes revisions older than the compaction revision. It calls `keyIndex.compact()` for each key, which maintains a map of available revisions to be kept.\\n\\n2. **Key-Value Pair Deletion** (`server/storage/mvcc/kvstore_compaction.go`): The `scheduleCompaction()` function performs batch deletion of actual key-value pairs from the backend database. It uses `kvindex.Compact()` to get the set of revisions to keep, then deletes all other revisions in batches (default 1000 keys per batch). The batching is configurable via `CompactionBatchLimit` and `CompactionSleepInterval` in `server/storage/mvcc/kvstore.go`.\\n\\n## Notification of Watch Streams Spanning Compacted Revisions\\n\\nWatch stream lifecycle management is implemented in `server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go` and `server/storage/mvcc/watcher_group.go`:\\n\\n1. **Watcher States**: The `watchableStore` maintains two groups of watchers:\\n   - `synced`: Watchers fully caught up with the current revision\\n   - `unsynced`: Slow watchers that are behind and need to catch up on events\\n\\n2. **Compaction Notification** (`server/storage/mvcc/watcher_group.go`, `chooseAll()` method): When syncing unsynced watchers, the `chooseAll()` function checks if any watcher's `minRev < compactRev`. For such watchers, it sends a `WatchResponse` with `CompactRevision` set to the compaction revision, marking the watcher as `compacted = true`. This causes the client to receive a cancellation with `compact_revision` indicating the event history has been compacted.\\n\\n3. **Event Synchronization Loop** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go`, `syncWatchersLoop()` and `syncWatchers()`): The background `syncWatchersLoop()` periodically calls `syncWatchers()` which:\\n   - Selects up to `maxWatchersPerSync` (512) unsynced watchers\\n   - Identifies the minimum revision across selected watchers\\n   - Retrieves events from the backend between minRev and current revision\\n   - Sends these events to watchers or marks them as \\\"victims\\\" if channel is blocked\\n   - Removes compacted watchers from the watcher group\\n\\n## Slow Watch Detection\\n\\nSlow watcher detection and handling involves:\\n\\n1. **Victim Processing** (`server/storage/mvcc/watchable_store.go`, `syncVictimsLoop()` and `moveVictims()`): When a watcher's channel is full and cannot receive an event, it's marked as a `victim` and moved to a victims batch. The `syncVictimsLoop()` runs continuously, attempting to resend events to victims with periodic retries (10ms delays).\\n\\n2. **Slow Watcher Gauge** (`server/storage/mvcc/metrics.go`): The metric `etcd_mvcc_slow_watcher_total` tracks the number of unsynced slow watchers. This is updated when watchers are moved between synced/unsynced states and when they become victims.\\n\\n3. **Watcher Lifecycle Transitions**:\\n   - During `notify()`, if a synced watcher's channel is full, it becomes a victim and is moved to `unsynced`\\n   - Victims are retried in `moveVictims()` which calls `w.send()` again\\n   - Once a victim successfully sends, it may be moved back to `synced` or `unsynced` based on whether its `minRev <= curRev`\\n   - The slowWatcherGauge is incremented/decremented as watchers transition between states\\n\\n4. **Compaction-Related Slowdown**: When a compaction revision passes a slow watcher's minimum revision, the watcher cannot catch up on the compacted events. The `chooseAll()` function detects this and immediately sends a compaction cancellation response, preventing indefinite slowdown.\\n\\nThe entire system is coordinated to ensure that compaction proceeds while notifying affected watchers efficiently, and slow watchers that fall behind are either brought current through event resynchronization or cleanly cancelled when their events have been compacted away.\"\n}\n",

(`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/periodic.go`): The `Periodic` compactor runs at configurable time intervals (default hourly). It maintains a sliding window of revisions recorded every 1/10th of the compaction period and compacts using the oldest revision in the window. The `Run()` method starts a goroutine that records revisions periodically and triggers compaction when the retention period is reached.\\n\\n2. **Revision-Based Compaction** (`server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/revision.go`): The `Revision` compactor triggers every 5 minutes by comparing current revision minus a retention number. The `Run()` method executes compaction when `currentRev - retentionCount > previousRev`.\\n\\nBoth are initialized by `server/etcdserver/api/v3compactor/compactor.go`'s `New()` function, which is called during server startup in `server/etcdserver/server.go` when `AutoCompactionRetention` is configured.\\n\\n## Compaction of Revision Indices\\n\\nThe actual compaction process involves two layers:\\n\\n1. **Key Index Compaction** (`server/storage/mvcc/index.go`): The `treeIndex.Compact(rev)` method iterates through all keys and removes revisions older than the compaction revision.
